Another Diplomatic Plan of President Hoover 56

Focusing on Disarmament Issues

Proceeding Simultaneously with the War Debt Suspension Plan

National News Agency, London, 7th. Washington has formally stated that US President Hoover intends to promote disarmament and the current war debt suspension plan simultaneously. Secretary of State Stimson's trip to Europe is for this reason. Recently, the Associated Press inquired about the attitudes of various countries in Geneva, Paris, Rome, Berlin, and London, and it seems that this move can receive the most favorable response. All parties say that in the past two weeks, President Hoover has transformed the atmosphere surrounding disarmament, and the situation of the Geneva Disarmament Conference next year has greatly improved. Because the suspension of reparations will reduce the budgetary income of some countries, they may be forced to reduce, or at least postpone, their naval shipbuilding programs and the expansion of land armaments. According to reliable sources, France and the United Kingdom are very willing to cooperate on general reductions and limitations of armaments, but claim that their reductions have already exceeded the limits that should be imposed in order to set an example. The British attitude was clearly expressed in Prime Minister MacDonald's speech in the House of Commons last week, and the leaders of the Conservative and Liberal parties, Baldwin and Lloyd George, both expressed their approval. Italy alone seems to be preparing to seek further reductions before the conference in February next year.

Reuters, Washington, 7th. The disarmament issue will be President Hoover's next diplomatic objective. President Hoover mentioned the arms issue when he recently gave a brief talk on the suspension of debts, so those responsible are convinced that President Hoover will take action.

German Prime Minister to Visit Italy as Well

National News Agency, Rome, 7th. US Secretary of State Stimson arrived in Naples at noon today. A representative specially dispatched by the Italian Foreign Ministry went to greet him and accompany him to the capital. Although the details of the US-Italian talks are not yet known, it is said that in addition to the much-discussed Hoover Plan, matters such as next year's disarmament conference will likely be subject to consultation, and there may also be intentions to mediate the points of contention between France and Italy that have prevented the conclusion of a Franco-Italian naval agreement.

National News Agency, Berlin, 7th. According to reports from Rome, German Prime Minister Brüning and Foreign Minister Curtius will visit Italy in mid-August, and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will visit Germany in return. If this is true, it would be Mussolini's first trip abroad in seven years. On the German side, Brüning has indeed invited the Italian Prime Minister to Germany, but it is feared that Mussolini will only follow convention and send Foreign Minister Grandi as his representative.

National News Agency, Rome, 7th. Italian Ambassador to Germany Ausonio Pironi visited Prime Minister Mussolini today. Pironi carried a handwritten letter from German Prime Minister Brüning, expressing his high regard for the Italian government's swift acceptance of the Hoover Plan, which gave the German people hope for recovery. British Ship from Shanghai to Kobe Has Passengers with Cholera 58

Telegraphic News Agency, Nagasaki, 8th. This morning, the British freighter "Rising" (transliteration) entered the port of Kobe with two Chinese passengers and one Indian passenger suffering from cholera. The ship came from Shanghai and is the first case of cholera this year.

Commentary

Advice to the Japanese and Koreans and Encouragement to the Chinese Regarding the Wanbaoshan Incident 59

In recent months, consultations between China and Japan regarding railways in the Northeast have been actively preparing for a formal meeting. The Chinese people are watching intently, hoping that in the future China and Japan can use sincerity to move from railway consultations to resolving all issues between China and Japan, supporting each other and jointly seeking the prosperity of both countries. Although there are rumors that the Japanese government and people have intense demands regarding our Northeast, we dare not believe that in today's autumn, when the winds and clouds over the Pacific are urgent and the slightest movement can shake the entire situation, the Japanese government would risk the disapproval of the world and easily disrupt peace on the Pacific. Especially since the bloodstains of the May 3rd Massacre have not yet dried and the rift between China and Japan still exists, each time Japan oppresses us, it only deepens the separation between the two peoples. The deterioration of the Chinese people's feelings towards Japan over the years is enough for the Japanese to consider deeply and at length. We even more dare not believe that the Japanese government would reenact a tragedy when the old pain of our people has not healed and the old hatred has not dissipated, forcing the relationship between the two countries to extremes. Unfortunately, like a bolt from the blue, the Wanbaoshan incident has occurred recently. We cannot help but feel grief, indignation, and regret over this.

In his memorial on an aggressive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia, Tanaka Giichi stated, "...The number of Koreans in the Three Eastern Provinces has reached nearly one million. This phenomenon means that the Empire's rights in Manchuria and Mongolia can be obtained without seeking them. It can truly be said that the nation has created immense happiness, and it adds countless forces to the Empire's defense and economy in Manchuria, showing immense hope in the governance of the Koreans." He also said, "On the one hand, we use the Koreans who have already naturalized to vigorously purchase rice paddies in Manchuria and Mongolia. On the other hand, credit cooperatives or banks, the Oriental Development Company, or the South Manchuria Railway Company in various places provide funds to Koreans with Chinese nationality, making them command posts for our economic invasion." He also said, "If the number of Koreans in Manchuria and Mongolia expands to over two million..." The Wanbaoshan incident was triggered by the Koreans forcibly reclaiming rice paddies and digging waterways, arousing fierce resistance from local farmers in our country. As of today, according to news from various sources, the case is expanding day by day, and the situation is becoming increasingly serious. Rioters in various parts of Korea have even brutally murdered our overseas Chinese, and the Japanese government has been dispatching troops and increasing its military presence in our Northeast, as if some major event is about to occur. Japanese Foreign Minister Shidehara even sent a telegram to the Japanese Consul General in Shenyang, saying, "...It is difficult to guarantee that the unfortunate incident of Showa 2 (i.e., the May 3rd Jinan Massacre) will not occur again... If the Chinese authorities ignore repeated warnings, the Japanese government, from the perspective of protecting Japanese residents in Manchuria, will have no choice but to take appropriate measures. As a result, an extremely serious situation may be brewed, which is unpredictable." (New Associated Press dispatch, June 3rd) From this, it can be seen that the various illegal actions of the Koreans are all planned and directed by the Japanese. We sincerely dare not predict to what extent the case will expand and become serious in the future. However, the Japanese people's violation of public reason and justice, and their showing the world their desperate actions with the dagger revealed at the end, make us recall the once-powerful Germany and Italy before the European War, and we cannot help but feel sorry for the Japanese and even more fear for them.

The Wanbaoshan incident, viewed on the surface, was caused by a minor matter. But looking into it, this case is actually the first shot of the Japanese's aggressive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia. We can easily deduce their consistent policy and planned preparation from the facts.

When Shidehara Kijūrō took office as Foreign Minister, his declared policy toward China was to be stable and restore the Chinese people's goodwill towards Japan, reversing the previous policy of violence and high-pressure tactics. Although his consistent execution of the continental policy was no different from before, his methods were indeed slightly more moderate. However, the ambitious politicians and military men of his country denounced him as weak and incompetent, humiliating to the Yamato race, and even called him a traitor in diplomacy. The whole country was clamoring, and criticisms came one after another. From top to bottom, they all regarded the so-called aggressive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia as a major issue, and there were arrogant remarks such as "We should sweep away the defects of diplomacy that only considers the faces of others, and we must have an active advocacy for the special status of Japan to the world." The government, under pressure from attacks by opposing parties within the country, in order to cater to the people and ease opposition, turned its aggression against our country into an aggressive one. This is the first remote cause of the Wanbaoshan incident. Since the Russian Revolution, the national system has been reformed, and its strength has been increasing day by day, far surpassing that of the past. The conflict of interests between the strong powers of Japan and the Soviet Union in our Northeast may re-ignite disputes at any time. The deterioration of the recent Japan-Soviet fisheries negotiations has made both countries feel uneasy. Japanese people with nervous disorders even said that the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan is tantamount to a plan to fight against Japan, and it is almost inevitable that Japan and the Soviet Union will re-ignite war. To prevent conflict between Japan and the Soviet Union, preparations must be made. And preparing for the Soviet Union must first conflict with our Northeast, so it is better to aggressively seize the Northeast and make arrangements first. Once the policy is determined, action follows. This is the second remote cause of the Wanbaoshan incident. Unemployment in Japan has been increasing recently. In order to alleviate the serious problem of domestic unemployment, they actively expel Koreans, who then flow into our Northeast, and transplant their nationals into Korean territory. According to recent reports, "When something happens in Japan, they use the Koreans as atoms and carry out military activities. They also use the pretext of crackdown to assist their actions." All these remarks, when verified with today's facts, are in perfect agreement. This is the third remote cause of the Wanbaoshan incident. From the above three causes, it can be known that the occurrence of the Wanbaoshan incident is the launch of the so-called "aggressive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia." Its inside story is certainly not as simple as the surface facts. As for the preparation for the implementation of the aggressive policy toward Manchuria and Mongolia, it is very clear from the appointment of Ugaki Kazushige as Governor-General of Korea, the appointment of Uchida Kosai as President of the South Manchuria Railway, and the increase of troops stationed in Korea and the change of the division stationed in our Northeast to a permanent station. Ugaki had served as Minister of the Army four times and had served as Acting Governor-General of Korea for four years. During the Kiyoura cabinet, he strongly advocated the speedy establishment of a continental policy. He also had considerable ambitions for the unification of policies toward Manchuria and Korea. Therefore, the Japanese government specially appointed him. In his speech after taking office, he said, "I served as Acting Governor-General of Korea for four years. At that time, I thought a lot about what I would try to do in the future. However, today's era is very different from that time. I plan to consider carefully and work hard to live up to expectations." The so-called "today's era is very different from that time" and "live up to expectations" all have meaning in the words, which are worthy of our deep thought. Moreover, his implementation of the military administration reorganization plan after taking office further proves that the Japanese government's appointment of Ugaki to govern Korea was a preparation for actual action against our Northeast. This is one. Uchida, as president, knew in detail how Japan's interests in our Northeast came about during the Russo-Japanese War. He was especially familiar with the situation in our country. At the same time, Uchida's views on the Manchurian question were consistent with Shidehara diplomacy. His three major principles for resolving the Northeast outstanding cases are: (1) Japan is responsible for maintaining the security of Manchuria. To prevent any unrest and shaking before it happens, the use of necessary means should be requested from the home government for prior decision under the understanding of the Chinese authorities. (2) The true mission of the South Manchuria Railway is to focus on the industrial development and cultural facilities of Manchuria and Mongolia. Japan should ensure its economic freedom in Manchuria based on its special relationship. However, this assertion of economic freedom does not intend to prevent the economic activities of China and third countries, and welcomes the economic activity of investment and trade by third countries to achieve equal opportunities and open doors. (3) Regarding railway policy, China and any third country are required to strictly abide by the main purpose of the Manchurian Rehabilitation Agreement. If China relies on the principle of coexistence and co-prosperity, taking the principle of profit sharing as a prerequisite, within the scope of not violating the aforementioned Rehabilitation Agreement, the laying of cultivating lines for existing trunk lines can be recognized. However, the South Manchuria Railway should adopt a dual-trunk line policy and require China to recognize Japan's right to build the Jilin-Huining Railway. These three major principles are designed to woo the great powers with the terms "open door" and "equal opportunity," and to deceive our country with the terms "coexistence and co-prosperity" between China and Japan. For what they call acquired rights in the Northeast, they take a tough stance, indicating that there is no room for concession, and their advocacy of using military force as a diplomatic backing is especially in line with the voices of the mad politicians in their country. It can be imagined that he is an old hand at diplomacy. We can also easily surmise Shidehara's deep consideration when recommending Uchida as the president of the South Manchuria Railway at this time. This is preparation two for aggressive action against our Northeast. According to a dispatch from the Tokyo One Day News Agency, the Council of Military Advisors submitted the plan for the establishment of a permanent division in Manchuria, decided by the Three Chiefs Meeting, for discussion. As a result, the original plan was approved, that is, one division from the mainland will be transferred to Manchuria as a permanently stationed division. The current system of stationing a division for a two-year rotation will be abolished. Also, regarding the discussion on increasing and strengthening the Korean army, Chief of Staff Kanaya said that the current Japanese national defense operations are based on continental operations, so in the event of an emergency, powerful troops should be urgently transferred to Manchuria and Mongolia to seize the initiative and make the battle situation develop favorably. The opportunity should be taken for General Ugaki to take office as Governor-General of Korea to decisively increase. Minister of the Army Minami also said that the purpose of increasing the number of troops stationed in Korea is not to maintain law and order, but to use troops for combat operations. As a result, it was proposed to (1) transfer one division stationed in the mainland to Korea, (2) send one brigade of resident troops to the mainland, and (3) establish an independent infantry unit in Korea in imitation of the Manchurian method. According to Japanese sources, the Japanese government, in view of the insufficient strength of the West Korean National Defense Force, has increased the planned garrison locations in West Korea, passing a resolution through the cabinet. One brigade headquarters each will be established along the Gyeongui Line and at the Daegu Station, garrisoning one regiment of infantry, plus three special corps teams of cavalry, artillery, and engineers. In addition, one brigade headquarters each will be established in Daejeon, garrisoning one regiment of infantry. One regiment of infantry will be stationed in Jeonju and Gwangju each. The 80th Infantry Regiment, originally stationed in Daegu, will be transferred to Uiju. Seeing this kind of hasty movement of dispatching troops and their so-called remarks of "national defense operations" and "continental operations," there is no doubt that they are preparing for combat. At the same time, the recent Japanese Air Force exercises in Dalian City further prove that they are not only preparing to aggressively invade our Northeast with political means, but have also prepared for aggressive military action. This is three. The Japanese people have already made a determination to invade our Northeast and are fully prepared. Then, the occurrence of the Wanbaoshan incident this time is by no means accidental, but inevitable. Our people must not ignore this point. (To be continued)

Important News

The Grave Situation of the Wanbaoshan Incident 60

Negotiations Repeatedly Fail

Japanese Actively Engage in Aggressive Behavior

Jilin People Have No Choice But to Act in Self-Defense

Japanese Police Use Rifles to Shoot at Jilin People

Jilin Correspondence: The case of Korean residents in Changchun digging up farmland in Wanbaoshan Town – according to correspondence three days ago – is a matter that has been repeatedly negotiated between China and Japan without satisfactory results. In the end, the provincial government insisted that the case should be resolved locally and need not be submitted to the province. As a result, the Japanese side exploited the Korean people even more severely, causing extreme anger among the Jilin people, which ultimately led to the unfortunate incident on the 2nd of this month. We will detail the past and present circumstances of this case as follows, and we urge the nation to pay attention to it.

The Origin of the Case: This case arose because Hao Yongde, the manager of the Changchun Rice Field Company, leased 500 *xiang* of raw and cultivated land in Wanbaoshan, Xiangsan District, Changchun County, from twelve people, including Xiao Hanlin, Zhang Hongbin, and Meng Zhaoshao, on April 16th of the 20th year of the Republic of China (1931), for a term of ten years. The contract stipulated that "This contract shall take effect on the date of approval by the county government; if the county government does not approve it, it shall be invalid." This contract was never formally approved by the Changchun County Government. At the same time, Hao Yongde sublet the aforementioned approximately 500 *xiang* of raw and cultivated land to nine Korean people, including Li Shengxun and Li Zaohe, for cultivation, also for a term of ten years. This contract was also not reported to Changchun County, and its validity is naturally out of the question. However, these Korean residents dug waterways on the land, diverting the Yitong River, occupying more than 20 *li* in length and 4 *zhang* in width of farmland along the way. This land belonged to another forty-one people, who had no contract with Hao Yongde or the Korean residents Li Shengxun. Moreover, this waterway diverting the Yitong River caused significant damage to the landowners and farmers. The soil dug out of the waterway was piled up on both sides to form embankments, about seven or eight *zhang* wide and more than 20 *li* long, destroying more than 400 *mu* of good farmland in total. The waterway passed through areas of cultivated land belonging to the people, dividing the cultivated land of each farmer into two sections. Furthermore, to divert the water from the Yitong River for irrigating the rice fields, a dam was built across the existing river, forcing water into the waterway. As a result of the dam blocking the river, the low-lying farmland on both sides of the river upstream, totaling about 2,000 *xiang*, would be flooded. Moreover, the area that Hao Yongde intended to rent for rice cultivation was at a higher elevation and had no drainage outlets, so the low-lying fields downstream, about several hundred *xiang*, would be flooded. The low-lying areas on both sides of the waterway would inevitably be flooded by rising river water, totaling about four or five thousand *xiang*. In addition, the Majiashaokou area of the river was a thoroughfare for travel between the east and west sides of the river. Due to the dam blocking the water in the river, the water level rose, and the old transportation routes between the east and west sides of the river were completely cut off. The river was an essential route for Changchun farmers to navigate and transport goods during the summer. The dam in the middle was over ten *zhang* high, obstructing public transportation routes in both counties. Hundreds of households living along the river, who relied on shipping for their livelihood, also suffered losses. The harm caused by this matter was so great that the local farmers, whose interests were directly affected, naturally opposed it. After the matter was reported by the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office to the province for instructions, the provincial government, considering that the Korean residents had entered the countryside without the permission of our authorities, which was contrary to the public agreement, ordered the county government on June 1st to send officials to cooperate with the county public security police to persuade the Korean residents to leave the country peacefully. However, the Korean residents refused to leave. The Public Security Bureau brought their leaders, Shen and eight others, to the county government, who claimed that they were ordered by the Japanese to come here to grow rice. On the 3rd, the head of the County Public Security Bureau and the captain of the guard led a team, together with Shen and others, to the Baishuichuzi area, where they expelled the Korean residents who were working. However, on the next

Page 11

Day, the Japanese ordered 100 Korean people to work in that area and sent five police officers to protect them, resulting in a confrontational situation, which is the origin of this case.

The Course of Negotiations 61

On June 3rd, Zhou Yuping, the head of the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office, sent a letter to the Japanese Consul Tadashiro, expressing his protest. The letter stated, "To the esteemed Consul, according to a report from Changchun County, there is a large group of about 200 Korean people, along with many Chinese laborers, in Wanbaoshan, Xiangsan District, forcibly digging up farmland and diverting water from the Yitong River. The Public Security Bureau has repeatedly ordered them to stop work, but they have not heeded the orders. According to the claims of more than 200 affected landowners, the Korean people are digging trenches about three *zhang* wide and three *zhang* deep, and more than 20 *li* long. This trench work is being carried out forcibly and is mostly completed. If the canal is completed, nearby farmland of more than 2,000 *xiang* will suffer from flooding in years of heavy rain. The Changchun County Government has, on the one hand, taken Hao Yongde, who recruited the Korean people, into custody pending investigation, and on the other hand, presented a report to the provincial government, which ordered the implementation of measures to stop the digging of the ditch and order the dissolution of the group. Shen Yongjun, Li Fushu, Jin Longzhu, Cui Xiangji, Zhu Rixing, and Li Xida, representing 200 Korean people, claimed to the Public Security Bureau on May 31st that they were willing to stop work and return to Changchun as a whole within two days. However, on June 1st, they reversed their statement and said that they could not stop work or leave the country even if it meant death. The Public Security Bureau selected Shen Yongjun, Li Fushu, Jin Longzhu, Cui Xiangji, Li Xitai, Jin Taijun, Sun Binghao, Li Xiangyang, Jiang Rirong, and Park Chenglong, ten people in total, and sent them to the county for detailed interrogation. They all claimed to be people engaged in reclaiming rice fields and claimed that the leaders, including Li Xichang, Park Lucheng, Zheng Ti Yu, Li Derui, Xu Longyun, Li Zaohe, Jin Dongshan, Shen Hengze, and Zheng Yuanze, all lived in Toudaogou. The digging routes were all instructed by these leaders. After being stopped by the government, they immediately stopped. The leaders claimed that the land occupied along the trench route had already been rented, so they continued to work. The Changchun County Government is still investigating. It has been reported that there are more than 100 Korean people still working and not heeding the orders. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to continue sending police teams to order the dissolution, the ten people, including Shen Yongjun, who were brought to the city, were sent to your office for interrogation, and it is requested that serious negotiations be conducted to severely punish Li Xichang and the other ten people who instigated the forced occupation of farmland and hard digging of ditches. As for the damage suffered by the affected landowners, once it is investigated, we will then request that you order compensation according to the amount. It is required that the planting of rice fields must be approved by the government. Hao Yongde rented farmland in Wanbaoshan, Xiangsan District, Changchun Township, to open up rice fields without formal government approval, and Li Xichang and the other nine people colluded secretly and incited a large group of Korean people to forcibly dig up other people's farmland for more than 20 *li*. In the future, nearby farmland of more than 2,000 *xiang* will be permanently damaged. The government's prohibition was ignored. It is truly disregarding the law. In addition to handing over the ten people, including Shen Yongjun, who were brought in, to your consulate for investigation, we hope that all the main criminals who instigated this will be severely punished according to the law to demonstrate the law and quell public anger. All losses of the households will be investigated later, and we will continue to negotiate the handling of the matter. We also hope that you will quickly inform us of the handling of your side." Since then, after consultations between China and Japan, it was agreed to send personnel to conduct an on-the-spot investigation of the truth, and then resolve the matter in a fair manner. During the investigation period, the Korean residents should immediately stop work. Our side should send personnel from the Changchun Municipal Office to investigate. As a result, it was determined that the rice field cultivation had not been approved by the government, and the damming of the river caused great damage. Based on this, negotiations with the Japanese consul continued. Unexpectedly, the Japanese consul still ordered the Japanese police to protect the Korean residents and continue the dam construction work. The Municipal Office sent another letter to the Japanese consul on the 12th, stating that the Japanese side should bear full responsibility for any disputes that may arise in the future. The original text is as follows: "To the esteemed Consul, Regarding the case of the joint dispatch of personnel by both sides to Wanbaoshan, Changchun County, to conduct an on-the-spot investigation of the cultivation of rice fields by Koreans and the resulting disputes with the majority of local landowners and farmers, which are likely to lead to conflict, according to the results of the joint investigation, the dug waterway is about 20 *li* long and is indeed forcibly occupied land that was not rented with consent. It is also planned to build a dam to cut off the Yitong River, which hinders shipping and transportation, and the farmland along the coast will be extensively flooded. The water diversion plan is absolutely unacceptable. The results of the investigation were copied and attached to the letter yesterday and sent to your consulate for reference. Our office's intention is that since the waterway plan is absolutely difficult to implement, there is no harm in changing the rented rice fields to dry rice cultivation and amending the contract with the landowners to avoid disputes and conflicts. If the waterway land cannot be rented properly and you are unwilling to cultivate the originally rented rice fields, you can abandon the rice field lease. Our office will order Hao Yongde, the counterparty to the contract currently detained in Changchun County, to compensate for the losses to show compassion. As for the current losses of the Korean people, your consulate mentioned a few days ago that they amounted to more than 3,000 Japanese yen. Our office will order Hao Yongde to be responsible for compensation, which is also reasonable. Last night, you told me at 10 p.m. that you intended to "make the Korean people, who are poor and pitiful, continue the river and dam work today to avoid delaying this year's farming" The official was deeply surprised when he heard this. The consular office was deeply concerned about the strong opposition from the majority of local landowners and farmers before the joint dispatch of personnel by both sides for investigation. He was afraid that conflicts would occur and that the police and army would join in succession, expanding the unfortunate dispute. Therefore, there was a joint on-the-spot investigation in order to seek a peaceful and proper solution. Before the investigation of this case began and was resolved, the police of both sides were withdrawn and all waterway work of the Koreans was stopped to avoid conflict, which was also a prerequisite for the resolution of this case agreed upon by both sides. Now, if we abandon the principle of peaceful and proper resolution and order the Korean people to continue the waterway work, it will be a fuse for expanding the conflict between the two sides, which is a violation of the original agreement and a breach of faith. First, the Korean people forcibly dug the waterway without the consent of the landowners concerned, which could still be attributed to the deceit of the counterparty to the contract and a good-faith interpretation. After the investigation, the facts were clear, but they still stubbornly carried out the work, which means that all previous work was done in bad faith, and the consular office is actually the initiator of the bad-faith behavior. Second, China and Japan are as close as lips and teeth. There are hundreds of thousands of Korean people who cultivate and engage in business in the three northeastern provinces. Our country treats them equally without any discrimination. Now, we are provoking the righteous resistance of Chinese landowners and farmers by supporting the Korean people's illegal behavior of forcibly occupying civilian land and cutting off shipping and transportation. Once a conflict occurs, the losses will be unimaginable. For the sake of peace, both sides should only solve the problem in good faith and fairness. Neither side should initiate meaningless provocations. If the Korean people continue to infringe on the inherent legal rights of the people and intend to insult them, an unexpected conflict is inevitable. Third, the local authorities of our two countries should only adhere to the principle of peaceful and proper handling of matters, and major matters can be turned into minor matters, and minor matters can be turned into nothing. If we go against this principle, unlimited disputes can occur anytime, anywhere, with anyone, and over anything. Now, by secretly supporting the illegal behavior of the Korean people, we are determined to infringe on the legitimate and inherent rights of Chinese landowners and farmers. On a small scale, the local masses will have a permanent sense of disgust towards your consular office. On a larger scale, it will also provoke a sense of disgust in the diplomatic relations between the Chinese and Japanese people, and your consular office is actually the initiator of this matter. I don't know what benefits you are doing this for. Fourth, I have a very good relationship with your consular office on weekdays, and the feelings between the people of China and Japan are becoming increasingly close. I really don't want the feelings between the people of China and Japan to deteriorate, and I especially don't want your consular office to be the initiator of the deterioration of the feelings between the people of China and Japan. I am making this final admonition, and I hope that you will consider it carefully. If you are unwilling to accept it and intentionally issue instructions to carry out malicious actions, your side shall bear full responsibility for all disputes and losses that may occur in the future. I hereby solemnly declare this and hope that you will give me your reply." After this letter was sent, the Japanese consul replied, still saying that the dam had not been started and that the digging of the ditch was harmless to farming. He also said that the Japanese police sent there were exclusively responsible for suppressing the Korean people. Zhou Yuping, the head of the Municipal Preparatory Office, continued to send a letter on the 17th, hoping that both sides would handle the matter fairly based on the facts of the meeting, but the Japanese side, led by the Consul General stationed in Shenyang, met with Zhang Zuoxiang, the chairman of the Jilin Provincial Government, and made representations, which were unsuccessful. At that time, the provincial government again insisted that the case should still be handled locally and was unwilling to take responsibility, which led to the delay until the end of June. The Korean farmers were increasingly anxious to build the dam because the harvest was delayed, while the Chinese people were increasingly resentful because of the heavy rain that caused the water in the paddy fields to overflow and flood the dry fields, and they saw that their fields were being damaged and that there would be no harvest in the autumn. They agreed with each other that if the Korean people continued to work, they would rise up to drive them away. They also sent representatives to urge the Municipal Office to make final representations to the Japanese consul, but the Japanese side had already decided on the policy of "local protection" and "promoting dam construction," and in the midst of the turbulent public sentiment, they increased the number of police officers and dispatched messenger pigeons to Wanbaoshan to strengthen protection. Our negotiations were without a trace, and the other party's progress was even more active. The people's hearts were indignant, as could be imagined. As a result, the conflict arose.

The Conspiracy of the Japanese 62

Before the Japanese sent additional police officers to Wanbaoshan Town, they purchased a large amount of food and transported it in advance, but they claimed that it was to supply the Korean people in the rice field area. According to the Japanese side, Tadashiro, the Japanese Consul stationed in Changchun, reported via messenger pigeon from the Japanese police protecting the Korean rice fields in Wanbaoshan, San District, that 500 to 600 Korean people in the rice field area lacked food and had no place to buy it. Even if they offered a high price, the nearby Chinese people would not sell it to them. Please purchase and transport it quickly for relief. After receiving the report, the Japanese Consul sent the Director of the Wubo Office to investigate and purchase a total of 270 bags of rice and six or seven boxes of other food. He sent four or five Japanese police officers to transport it to Misha Station via the China Eastern Railway, and then hired Chinese carts to transport it to the rice field area in Wanbaoshan, etc. However, when they arrived at the station and were about to unload, all the Chinese cart drivers refused to be hired when the Japanese police came out to hire carts. Even if they doubled the freight, they would not transport it. The public anger was aroused, and the people's hearts were aligned. It was found that Misha Station was more than 30 *li* away from Wanbaoshan. Even if there were no carts available, it had to be transported. Helpless, the Japanese police escorting the goods ordered the Korean people to carry them on their backs and shoulders and transport them on foot. The Korean people were slow to carry heavy loads, and the Japanese police whipped and beat them. The Korean people were angry but dared not speak, shedding tears and presenting a miserable sight. It took two or three days to complete the transportation. Later, the Japanese police transported more than 5,000 bundles of willow branches and more than 500 earth-carrying baskets, and supervised and directed the Korean people to continue digging ditches to divert water and building dikes and forts, actively working and setting a deadline of July 5th to complete all the work. They also forced the Korean people to sow rice seeds on the wasteland owned by the Chinese people, covering the fields. It is difficult to speculate on their intentions. According to the victims in the area who came to the city, it is generally observed that the Japanese police are forcing the sowing of seeds in order to expand the demand for compensation when negotiations fail.

The Anger of the Farmers 63

The Chinese people in Wanbaoshan Town, seeing that the Korean people's work of planting rice and building weirs and digging trenches was not stopped, and that the County Government and the Municipal Diplomatic Office were unable to stop it, and that it would be difficult to achieve victory without the self-defense of the masses, specially convened a support meeting for the resistance of the Korean people's construction of weirs on June 30th, gathering the affected landlords and nearby farmers in Wanbaoshan Town. More than 500 people attended the meeting, which was chaired by Sun Langxuan. He reported on the purpose of the meeting and the course of the negotiations, and described the situation of the Japanese police supervising and directing the Korean people to carry out dike construction and sowing on the land. Then, representatives from various villages expressed their opinions. All the people were extremely indignant. Some advocated using force to expel the Korean people, some advocated self-defense and resistance, and some advocated that all villages should unite and take action to fill up the ditches and destroy the dikes dug by the Korean people. As a result, a president and vice president, and an executive director and vice executive director were elected, along with 30 executive members, who were responsible for handling the affairs of the support association. They were divided into four departments: documentation, investigation, publicity, and accounting, and it was decided to submit a petition urging diplomatic officials and the county magistrate to negotiate effectively. In addition, the executive members would unite with the affected villages and assign workers from each household to automatically fill up the ditches and destroy the dikes as a final struggle to achieve their final self-defense. The director of the County Farmers' Association also joined with leaders from all walks of life to launch a municipal diplomatic support association, holding preparatory meetings from June 30th to July 1st to study ways to deal with the Sino-Japanese rice case negotiations, and formulating regulations for each department, including investigation, publicity, documentation, research, and executive affairs. The organization is currently being implemented. Once it is in place, a formal establishment meeting will be held regularly to elect the chairman, committee chairman, and heads of each department, who will be responsible for assisting in the rice case negotiations and serving as a backing for the government. After this, whenever there is a local Sino-Japanese negotiation event, the Changchun Municipal Diplomatic Support Association will also assist in the investigation, propose suggestions, and submit requests to the Diplomatic Office to submit protests based on them.

The Circumstances of the Conflict 64

On the 2nd of this month, the farmers of Wanbaoshan Town, acting in self-defense, gathered four to five hundred people to fill up the trenches, but the Japanese police openly fired live ammunition at our farmers. The farmers jumped into the trenches to avoid the shots. The Japanese police fired 38 shots and stopped firing when they saw that our farmers did not retaliate. At that time, the head of the Tian Branch of the police station in the county-administered San District came out to mediate and temporarily persuaded the farmers to return. This scene of martial arts drama temporarily came to a stop. At that time, after our government heard the news, it made representations to the Japanese Consulate. The following are excerpts from two letters sent by the Municipal Office to the Japanese Consul: (1) To the esteemed Consul, Your official document No. 50 of today has been read and understood. The Korean people of Wanbaoshan have violated current laws and regulations and engaged in illegal acts without agreed contracts, infringing on the inherent legal rights of farmers and obstructing shipping and transportation. On June 8th, both sides agreed on a method to investigate and resolve the matter, with the withdrawal of the Japanese police and the cessation of the Korean people's work as prerequisites for resolving the case. However, after the fact-finding investigation was completed, on the 12th of the same month, your side sent plainclothes Japanese police to the scene to cover the Korean people's continued digging of waterways and building of dams across the river, violating good faith and deliberately engaging in malicious acts to infringe on the inherent legal rights of landowners and farmers. The farmers were overwhelmed with hatred and could not bear it, and were forced to automatically restore the original state and implement their legitimate means of self-defense. The motives were described in detail in official letter No. 183 on June 27th, as were the actual circumstances described in this letter of yours, in which the chief of our Second Branch went to suppress the situation and could not stop it. You should be aware that violent acts of aggression are not a good plan. The police officers sent by your side should be withdrawn in full to avoid conflict. If they are not withdrawn immediately, your side shall bear full responsibility for all conflicts and incidents that may occur, in accordance with this office's official letter No. 159 of June 12th. I hereby solemnly declare this again. As for the issue of compensation for damages between the parties concerned, once your police officers have been completely withdrawn, both sides will resolve the matter fairly and appropriately in accordance with the law and reason, based on the requests of the parties concerned. I have sent this letter to you in response to the previous correspondence. This is addressed to Tadashiro, the Japanese Consul stationed in Changchun. (2) To the esteemed Consul, According to a telephone report from the Second and Third Branches of Changchun County at noon today, this morning, the farmers of Wanbaoshan continued to gather to restore the original state of the river ditch. The Japanese police fired shots and implemented shooting, firing a total of 38 bullets. The farmers immediately jumped into the trenches, and the crowd was extremely indignant, each wanting to seize weapons to resist. They were repeatedly dissuaded and temporarily returned home to await a negotiated solution. Fortunately, no incident was triggered. Please make serious representations to the Japanese Consul to withdraw all the Japanese police immediately to avoid conflict. Your side has violated the previous agreement by continuing to send police, which is already a violation of good faith. However, when the farmers took legitimate means of self-defense and acted to restore the original state, the police sent by your side dared to fire live ammunition, which is extremely barbaric and unreasonable. Your side should quickly withdraw all the police officers who were sent immediately and give the police officers appropriate punishment to avoid further complications and increase all the responsibilities that your side should bear. This is what I hope for, and I hope that you will give me your reply on the handling of the matter. This is addressed to Tadashiro, the Japanese Consul stationed in Changchun. The Japanese Consul ignored both of the above letters and continued to diligently carry out the deployment of troops. According to people from Wanbaoshan, as of the evening of the 2nd, there were already 58 armed Japanese police officers in the area, setting up checkpoints and patrolling, which was extremely serious. Furthermore, at about 9 a.m. on the 3rd, the Japanese side sent 16 Japanese police officers and two baggage carts loaded with military tents and military food, two machine guns, and some ammunition, and dug trenches in places such as Majiashaokou. The situation was turbulent, as if facing a great enemy. According to people in the area, when the Japanese police and the farmers clashed and the Japanese police fired, more than 30 Korean people who were aware of the situation took the opportunity to escape. It can be seen that the Korean people are unwilling to be puppets of the Japanese. However, the Japanese are monitoring the situation very strictly and are refusing to back down. It is still difficult to predict how the situation will develop in the future. (July 3rd)

Summary Execution of Bandit Division Commander by Hankow Garrison Headquarters 65

Hankow Dispatch: The Wuhan Garrison Headquarters summarily executed a bandit division commander, Wu Ying, at Liudu Bridge on the 6th. The charges are as follows. The Garrison Headquarters Intelligence Office delivered the red bandit's pseudo-division commander Wu Ying, also known as Wu Qingsong, requesting interrogation. After investigation by the Garrison Headquarters Military Law Office, the bandit Wu Ying confessed to joining the Red Party, serving as the commander of the Bandit Army's First Independent Division, stationed in Zhengdaohu, Hanchuan. He had engaged in battle with the local militia. Recently, he was appointed by the pseudo-government to come to Hankow to gather information and re-establish Wuhan organizations. The investigation revealed that the bandit Wu Ying was a graduate of a military academy and had served as a soldier. He colluded with bandits and held an important position in the bandit army. His crimes are severe and unforgivable. In accordance with Article 1, Section 4 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Those Who Endanger the Republic of China, he is sentenced to death as a warning to others. It is hereby announced that the bandit Wu Ying has been verified, bound, and taken to the execution ground for summary execution by firing squad for all to know. This announcement is made.

At the same time, Bing Chengyanxiu, a soldier who stole and sold firearms, was also executed by firing squad. In addition, the Garrison Command beheaded Zhang Ruiting, who supplied ammunition to the bandits, Zhou Peitang, who looted, burned, and killed, Wang Jianqing, who kidnapped for ransom, and Wang Yawa, Qiu Yushan, Chen Yushan, Liu Changgeng, Gong Chong, and eight others who robbed the Rongfeng Store. Furthermore, Xiang Zhongfa, a leader of the Red Bandits, has been active in Hubei for many years. Following his execution in Shanghai, the Red Bandit Central Committee issued an order to various regions to hold a large anti-white demonstration on the 7th in commemoration. Upon receiving this information, the Garrison Headquarters ordered the Garrison Command to strengthen defenses. Therefore, Wuhan was under undeclared martial law on the 7th, and emergency inspections were conducted at various street corners. (July 7th)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 66

Handling of the Case of the Wanted Bandit Taibao Ashu, Following the Delivery of Xia Zexian et al. to the Ministry: The wanted bandit Xia Zexian, who was previously on the wanted list of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters, was discovered by the Water Police First District Chief Xu Pucheng in Shanghai. Detectives were dispatched to arrest him, and he was brought back to the Minhang District office for interrogation. He confessed to joining the Communist Party and participating in gang robberies. He was registered with Luo Fugen and both were escorted to the Headquarters for interrogation. Upon arrival in Songjiang yesterday, the Headquarters Secretary Zheng interrogated Xia Zexian. His confession differed slightly from the District office. He stated that he was forty-seven years old, from Zhangze Town, joined the Kuomintang in the 13th year, was in the Second District Party office, in the 15th year he was an inspector for the Water Police Bureau, and in the 16th year he worked at the Changshu Public Security Bureau. Last May, he was introduced to the Communist Party by Zhou Zhigang and had no work. He did not know the bandit leaders Taibao Ashu, Zhuluo A'mei, etc. Luo Fugen confessed that he was from Zhangyan and was a cook at a Shanghai yarn factory in January. In February, he was introduced to work as a cook for Li Wenjun with a monthly salary of eight yuan. Because Gu Xiao'an was also cooking together, they took a photo together and he was unaware that Gu was a bandit. He asked for leniency. The interrogating officer found that the bandit's confessions were cunning and did not match the confessions made at the District office, and further investigations will be conducted to make a decision. According to reports, Xia Zexian was reported last year for his secretive behavior and was investigated by the County Party Headquarters and his party membership was revoked. Since then, he has stayed in various places and dared not return home.

Suzhou 68

Request to Revise Sino-Japanese Silk Tax: The Wuxian Association for Promoting National Goods, in view of the repeated oppression of Chinese commerce by imperialism and the constraints of unequal treaties, the long-term stagnation of domestic goods, the influx of foreign goods, and the deep suffering of merchants and civilians, is investigating that the original Japanese tax rate for Chinese silk sold to Japan and Korea is as high as 70% of the value, while the tax rate for Japanese goods sold to China is only 8%. The two sides compared are extremely unfair. It is urgent to take advantage of the Sino-Japanese treaty revision period to propose revisions in order to meet the principle of mutual benefit and equality. Therefore, it is specially recommended that the county chamber of commerce send a letter to the Sino-Japanese Agreement Tariff Rate Research Committee and a circular to related industrial groups to send representatives to convene public discussions on a regular basis.

Wuxi 69

Xue Jingqiu Falsely Accuses Good People of Theft: A woman from the Nan Shuangmiao Township, Madam Xi Yang, because her husband Xi Jinbao was falsely accused of theft by Xue Jingqiu, was detained and imprisoned. Recently, Jinbao died of illness in prison. His funeral was simple, and his family was destitute. He had an octogenarian father and a six- or seven-year-old orphan. The Entire Shili Datang is Submerged: There have been three days of heavy rain in this county, and the river has risen by three or four feet. The low-lying fields have become swamps, and the roads in the low-lying areas of the city and countryside are submerged. The Beitang area is a district where rice shops gather. Wheat has been on the market for days. The wheat collected by each shop during the day is piled up at the entrance of the courtyard. Unexpectedly, the river surged the night before, causing the wheat piled up in the courtyard to be submerged. When it was noticed at dawn, rescuers salvaged it, but the loss was huge. The road from Beitang Wuqiao to Gaoqiao, which is about ten miles long, is an important road along the canal. Now the road surface is submerged in water, two feet deep. Pedestrians detour and take the railway.

Because of playing around for a long time, the bandits grew bigger. Wuchang 76

Strange Case in Wuchang: He Chengli, the son of the gardener He Bingchen, suddenly died on the 4th of this month in Hejia Vegetable Garden on Changhu Dike near Ziyang Bridge in Wuchang. It is said that he was killed by a monster. For a time, the city was full of rumors. After a detailed examination by the court, the cause of his death was unknown. The details of this case are described in detail on the left. The gardener He Bingchen has been working at the Xianning Station of the Yuehan Railway. The several acres of fields at home are all entrusted to his wife Li, his son Chengli, and his wife's brother Li Haishan for management. Recently, because the garden was full of melons and fruits, fearing theft, He's son and uncle Li Haishan built a shed in the garden to guard it. At 9 pm on the 4th of this month, they went to the garden together. He had just entered the door when he fell to the ground immediately. Li felt something pounced on him and also fainted. After a while, he woke up and took He to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but he was beyond saving. The Wuchang Local Court was reported and sent personnel for examination. It was found that the chest meat of the deceased He Chengli had been completely removed, the internal organs could be seen, and the throat had also been grabbed. No drop of blood could be found, and there was no blood at the injury site. Li Haishan was examined and found to have scratches on the right cheek of his face and slight injuries to both arms. It was neither human harm nor animal injury. The court summoned and interrogated twice, but no clues could be found. According to Prosecutor Chen, who is in charge of this case in the county, the court has never handled such a strange case, but it cannot be attributed to monsters. He is now studying it in detail in order to find the truth.

Letter from Li Jinfang 77

I read in the Zhenjiang Dispatch column on the third page of your newspaper on July 8 that more than a dozen county magistrates selected in the second Jiangsu Provincial Examination, including Li Jinfang, prepared a briefing and visited the Provincial Chairman and the Director of the Civil Affairs Department to request an increase in subsidies. Jinfang was indeed selected as a county magistrate in the second examination, but after reporting a major financial corruption case for the second time during his tenure in Liyang County, he was illegally suspended from his post by the Jiangsu Provincial Government. For months, he has been fighting hard for justice and is fundamentally opposed to the Jiangsu Provincial Government. He disdains to accept any subsidy from them and has no reason to prepare a briefing to request an increase. This concerns personal integrity, so I request that your newspaper publish it in the Letters to the Editor column to correct it. I am very grateful. Li Jinfang, July 8.

Local News

Generalissimo Memorial Pavilion Various Boy Scout Troops Donate Actively 81

Jiangsu Province's 20th Year Education Expenditure Budget (4) Shi Zhang 82

(4) Reality and Possibility of Total Revenue

The total budget for this year is 4,880,000 yuan. Numerically speaking, it is 16,552 yuan less than last year (see the report in this newspaper on July 6). But in reality, it is not so. It is also permissible to say that it has increased a lot compared with last year. For example, the total expenditure of educational institutions this year is 4,491,155 yuan, while it was 4,150,472 yuan last year (see the report in this newspaper on July 7). Isn't this a clear increase of 340,683 yuan? However, the reserve fund and the temporarily allocated temporary expenses are not as much this year as last year. (This year's reserve fund is 95,388 yuan and the separately allocated temporary expenses are 293,457 yuan, totaling 388,845 yuan. Last year's reserve fund was 397,190 yuan and the separately allocated 348,890 yuan, totaling 746,080 yuan, a difference of 357,235 yuan. This difference is precisely the source of the increase of 340,683 yuan in the expenses of educational institutions this year.) However, the amount of these two types of funds has no deep relationship with the expenses themselves. Because the actual amount of income often cannot follow the budget, it has become an unavoidable phenomenon. Therefore, the amount of the reserve fund and the separately allocated fund naturally has sufficient elasticity. Even if the amount is as per the plan, in fact, when faced with a deficit, it is still set aside and attempts are made to use it. The reserve fund and the separately allocated fund in the 19th year totaled 746,080 yuan. Numerically speaking, it is not too much, but the actual temporary expenses only accounted for 180,000 yuan, only a quarter, and it was allocated after the end of the 19th year (details will be given later). It is not yet known when each school can receive this fee. This is clear proof of its elasticity. As for expenses, they are paid on time and no shortage is allowed, which is rigid and cannot be reduced unless absolutely necessary. This year's budget has reduced the elastic temporary expenses by 357,235 yuan, and at the same time, it has increased the rigid recurring expenses by 3,40,683 yuan according to the degree of reduction. This is an improvement in the budget and a responsible representation by the educational administrative authorities. The above-mentioned budget for this year does not actually reduce, which is the reason. After explaining the practicality of this year's budget, I will further talk about its possibility, that is, whether this budget can be fully realized this year. This is a very important point. The implementation of the budget in the past few years has inevitably suffered from the problem of false income and real expenditure. The constant depletion of funds in the 18th year led to the misappropriation of 540,000 yuan from the income of the 19th year. The repeated and delayed payments in the 19th year caused repeated meetings and expressions by the education staff association. These are the results of false income and real expenditure. Of course, the real expenditure is appropriate and there is no problem with it. The only problem is the "false" in the income. If the income can be real, the expenditure can also be real. Otherwise, if the number is false, then the expenditure will also be false, and various unexpected disputes will follow. So, can the income of this year's budget be "real"? To answer this question, we must first look at the contents listed in the budget, and especially look at the contents and comparison of the income listed in recent years. The income budgets for the past three years are listed below.

Item Budget for the 18th Year Budget for the 19th Year Budget for the 20th Year

Land Tax Grain Tribute 2,200,000 yuan 2,480,000 yuan 2,500,000 yuan

Slaughter Tax 1,200,000 yuan 1,280,000 yuan 1,300,000 yuan

Tuition and Accommodation 152,980 yuan 171,980 yuan 180,000 yuan

Provincial Subsidy 75,000 yuan 375,000 yuan 300,000 yuan

Ministry of Finance Returns Old Debts 200,000 yuan 600,000 yuan

Old Debt Land Tax Collection 300,000 yuan 300,000 yuan

Increased Revenue from Management Office 89,572 yuan 89,572 yuan

Total 4,017,552 yuan 4,896,552 yuan 4,880,000 yuan

Based on the table above, a rough calculation can be made. (1) In the 18th year, 540,000 yuan from the income of the 19th year was misappropriated, so the actual income for that year was at most 3,500,000 yuan. (2) In the 19th year, although the time has passed, the income and expenditure have not ended. In fact, each school's expenses have only been paid up to the first half of May. In the previous year, there were still one and a half months (up to June) owed, with an average of 400,000 yuan per month and one and a half months amounting to 600,000 yuan. Then, the amount received was at most 4,300,000 yuan. (In fact, it is absolutely impossible to receive this amount). Adding the 540,000 yuan misappropriated from the 18th year, then the shortfall for the previous year, as of this time, should be more than one million. The amount of one million is huge. (3) If there are other ways to make up for the above-mentioned deficit, then even if this year's income is completely real, it cannot be free from its constraints and influence. What's more, whether this year's income is real or not is still a problem. Therefore, the reporter is not optimistic about this year's budget.

Now, let's take a step back and just predict the income situation for this year's budget, and explain each income item one by one.

(I) 田賦 Appropriation of Funds 83

This year's allocation is listed as 2,500,000 yuan, which is less than the previous two years (the previous year was 2,500,000 yuan [including both land tax and old arrears collection], and the year before that was 2,780,000 yuan). This is naturally because there was an understanding of the unreliability of previous collections and preparations were made accordingly. It has been determined that the allocation of Jiangsu Province's education funds from land tax stems from the nationalization of the cigarette tax funds that were originally used for education. Previously, a "dispatch of funds" method was used, initially set at 1,800,000 yuan, which was subsequently gradually increased. However, the funds dispatched to various counties often fell short of the required amount, so a "appropriation" method was adopted (that is, 4 jiao were extracted from each shi of Cao rice regular tax, 2 jiao and 2 fen from each liang of Mang silver regular tax, and 2 jiao and 5 fen from each liang of Mang silver provincial tax). After many twists and turns, the provincial government's education department, finance department, education funding committee, and education funding management office negotiated back and forth dozens of times. From March of the 17th year, until the 292nd meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Government on May 9th of the 19th year, it was resolved that "starting from the Cao Mang tax collection of the 18th year, the distribution will be implemented, and the Finance Department will be ordered to comply; old arrears will be cleared separately." The "distribution" method was thus finally implemented. In the past year or so, the amounts remitted by various counties have gradually improved. In the first year of implementation, the reported amounts were inevitably slightly inferior. This year is considered the second year of implementation, and it should be better. Therefore, this income is expected to be reliable, or it may even exceed the amount of 2,500,000 yuan. Didn't the above mention that the budgeted amounts for the previous two years were higher than this year? Furthermore, on March 14th of this year, the Finance Department sent a letter to the management office and funding committee stating, "After investigating the special education funds appropriated from land tax, which are extracted from our department's collection of Ding Cao and reed taxes on a per-liang and per-shi basis, the standard for budgeted income should be calculated based on the average of the actual collection amounts of Liang and Shi from the autumn surveys of the past three years, and then converted at 4 jiao and 7 fen per Liang and 1 yuan and 4 jiao per Shi. According to this standard, the annual special education funds appropriated should be approximately 3.22 million yuan. However, the budget for the 19th year only lists 2.78 million yuan, a difference of more than 400,000 yuan, which is inconsistent with the overall land tax amount. Now that we are handling the budget for the 20th year, we are specially listing the average actual collection amounts from the autumn surveys of the past three years and the special education funds that should be appropriated (see below) and attaching them for your review. Please list them as the budget for the 20th year based on the amounts listed in the list, so as to avoid repeating the mistakes of the previous year." The detailed items are as follows:

(A) The average actual collection of land Ding tax for three years is 2,550,625 liang, and 4 jiao and 7 fen are allocated per liang, totaling 1,198,793 yuan.

(B) The average actual collection of Cao rice for three years is 1,400,132 shi, and 1 yuan and 4 jiao are allocated per shi, totaling 1,960,185 yuan.

(C) The average actual collection of reed tax for three years is 147,922 liang.

4 jiao and 7 fen are allocated per liang, totaling 69,523 yuan.

The total of the above three items that should be allocated is 3,228,501 yuan. Judging from this, it is possible that this income will exceed the budgeted amount by a certain amount. However, land tax is directly proportional to the harvest. If this year's harvest is not very good, there may not be much hope for excess revenue. However, there can be a considerable degree of certainty regarding the listed amounts.

(II) Slaughter and Tooth Tax 84

There has been little increase in recent years, and the collected amount is quite reliable. The surplus bonus for the tooth tax in March of this year reached more than 12,470 yuan, which gives an idea of its surplus situation.

(III) School Accommodation Fees 85

The amount is reliable and there are no problems. However, various schools are often unwilling to remit the funds as required, wanting to retain them for other uses. If in the future we can achieve the point where the reported amount matches the remitted amount, that will be sufficient.

(IV) Provincial Treasury Subsidy 86

This subsidy can be considered an additional income. In fact, isn't the 2 to 3 million yuan appropriated from land tax originally funds belonging to the provincial treasury? Because the provincial budget has gradually increased in recent years, while the dispatched and appropriated funds have a fixed amount and cannot be easily increased, and the education undertaking is continuing to develop, this special subsidy has been provided. It is estimated that half was received in the 17th year, one-third was received in the 18th year, and the full amount will be gradually received in the 19th year. It is expected that there will be no further arrears within this year.

(V) Repayment of Old Arrears by the Ministry of Finance 87

The 200,000 yuan from last year has not yet been received, and this year it has even increased to 600,000 yuan, which is feared to be even more hopeless. It is heard that when the education funding committee discussed this year's budget, everyone believed that there was no certainty at all and did not know how to ensure that the full amount could be received in the future.

In summary, the practicality and possibility of this year's budget are greater than last year's. If the situation can be stable and harvests are bountiful, then the degree of nominal income and actual expenditure can hopefully improve. Is this the new dawn of Jiangsu's educational future? (To be continued)

World Boxing Championship Double Title Case: New York Starts Anew 92

Schmeling and Walker to Face Off on the 22nd of This Month

Both Sides Claiming World Championship

New York. Jack Schmeling and Michael Walker, recognized by New York as contenders for the World Heavyweight Boxing Championship, signed a contract today to compete on the 22nd of this month at the Ebbetts Field in Brooklyn. Walker, the undefeated American Middleweight Champion, has retired from boxing and is now participating in heavyweight competitions to contend with Schmeling. The victor of the contest will be recognized by New York State as the World Heavyweight Boxing Champion, turning the championship into a double title case. The New York boxing community has consistently refused to acknowledge Michael Schmeling's retaking of the title on July 3rd.

The East China Sports Company Sponsors the Chinese Student Shanghai Tennis Championship 96

Registration Begins Immediately, Deadline is Noon on the 18th

Singles and Doubles Matches Held Every Other Day Starting from the 20th

The East China Sporting Goods Company, with the aim of promoting sports, has been sparing no effort in encouraging amateur sports since its establishment, in addition to selling various sports equipment. As the tennis season is approaching, and seeing that there are many masters in various schools in Shanghai, although there are various competitions at ordinary times, they cannot be brought together due to different organizations or groups. The only open competition is the Chinese Open Tennis Tournament held by the Chinese Athletic Association. However, it should be known that the more competitions there are in sports, the more intense the competition will be, and the skills will become more refined as a result. Looking back at various countries in Europe and the United States, the number of competitions held each year is countless. Even in New York State in the United States, there are dozens of competitions in one season. No wonder they have always held the leading position in the world. Even in nearby Japan, its rapid progress is truly astonishing, and it is also the result of rigorous training and fierce competition. Recently, Canadian Davis Cup representatives Andrew and Duff returned to Shanghai from a competition in Japan. They talked about the progress of their skills and the number of talented people in various schools, which should be a serious warning to our people. The East China Sporting Goods Company also firmly believes that to cultivate talents, one must start from the schools. Therefore, it has decided to hold the Chinese Student Shanghai Tennis Championship. Any student studying at any school in Shanghai (including those who have graduated this year but have not held positions in institutions) can join, regardless of whether it is a university or middle school. Students from other cities who are currently in Shanghai can also participate. This time, the company has also negotiated with the British Sporting Goods Company, A. G. Spalding and Bros (Br Ltd), to donate several Spalding Top Flite rackets as prizes. These rackets are specially made in England, and the weight and handle size can be selected by the individual to ensure suitability. The racket will also be printed with the championship competition and the individual's name as a souvenir. As for the balls used in the competition, they will all be provided by the East China Sporting Goods Company and will all be Spalding brand, using new balls each time. There are also other prizes, which are still in progress. In short, this competition is a new initiative in the tennis world. Who knows if future talents for our country will not be produced from this? The registration location is the East China Sporting Goods Company, 10 Nanjing Road Central Road. Registration will be open from today until noon on the 18th. The competition is scheduled to begin on the 20th, with singles and doubles matches held every other day, and will last approximately three weeks. The selection of doubles partners is up to the individuals and is not limited to the same school. In the future, the heroes of various schools will gather together and there will be a fierce competition. It is hoped that all sectors will provide enthusiastic support and participate in this grand event. The competition rules are attached below.

Rules for Singles and Doubles Matches 97

(1) This competition is sponsored by the Shanghai East China Sporting Goods Company and is named the Chinese Student Shanghai Tennis Championship. A separate committee will be formed to handle it. (2) All Chinese students who are currently studying, or graduates of this summer who have not held positions in institutions, can register to join the competition with appropriate proof.

(3) This competition can only be held if there are at least 20 or more participants.

(4) All competition balls will be new Spalding balls, provided by the East China Sporting Goods Company.

(5) The prizes for each competition will be donated by the East China Sporting Goods Company. This year's prizes are as follows:

Doubles 98

First place: Each person will receive a Spalding Top Flite racket, strung with the best British line, worth 80 yuan (this prize is donated by British Spalding)

Second place: Each person will receive a Spalding Top Flite racket, strung with Singapore line, worth 40 yuan (this prize is donated by East China Company)

Singles 99

First place: A Spalding Top Flite racket, strung with the best British line, worth 80 yuan (this prize is donated by British Spalding)

Second place: A Spalding Top Flite racket, strung with good British line, worth 60 yuan (this prize is donated by British Spalding)

Third place: A Spalding Top Flite racket, strung with Singapore line, worth 40 yuan (this prize is donated by East China Company)

(6) The competition venue will be held on the grass courts of the China Tennis Club.

(7) Each competition will use a knockout system, but in the final rematch of the singles competition, a single round-robin system will be used to determine the ranking.

(8) In each competition, except for the rematch and final, a best-of-five-sets system will be used, and the rest will use a best-of-three-sets system to determine the winner.

(9) Players must compete according to the scheduled date and time. The competition must not be delayed or postponed for any reason. If a player does not appear within 15 minutes of the scheduled time, it will be considered a forfeit.

(10) In the event of inclement weather or rain, each participant should call the East China Company between 12:00 pm and 1:00 pm to inquire whether the competition will be held (telephone 15612).

(11) Registration for the competition is scheduled to begin on July 20th, from today until noon on the 18th. At the time of registration, a registration fee of one yuan per person per competition should be paid, and a school certificate should be brought along.

(12) All matters concerning the competition shall be handled and executed by the committee.

Ministry of Communications Took Over Yangtze Wharf Yesterday 104

Also Detained a Small Steamer

The Outstanding Rent Will Still be Prosecuted According to Law

The Japanese firm Ocean Society rented the Ministry of Communications' property, the Yangtze Wharf in Pudong, but refused to pay rent. After the Ministry of Communications sent a representative, Xu Shidan, to Shanghai, in addition to formally notifying the general manager of the Ocean Society, Mr. Chuan Yue, by official letter a few days ago, and personally meeting with the manager in the morning to request the return, he also went to receive it yesterday afternoon at 2:00 pm, accompanied by the Navigation Bureau's technicians Zeng Shoulian and Ding Yanling, staff Xu Yiqun, Cai Yun, Feng Heqin, and Chen Weixian, as well as Tang Jinghuan, the chief of the Sixth Precinct of the Third District of the Public Security Bureau in Pudong, leading five policemen, and Mr. Einler, a surveyor from the American Shipping Company recognized by the American government. When Representative Xu and others first arrived, the wharf manager, a Japanese named He Zhishang, refused to hand it over. After the Japanese person inquired with the manager by telephone, he handed it over. Xu and others, along with the notary public, American surveyor Einler, inquired about each warehouse, etc., and confirmed that there were no goods stored in any of them, and then sealed them with tape, ready for inspection today. In addition, the company had a small steamer when renting the wharf. Because the Ministry of Communications' representative did not see the original steamer, they detained a small steamer of about 45 feet moored at the wharf yesterday for compensation. Moreover, Representative Xu saw that the small steamer did not have any flag hanging, so he put up the Chinese national flag and hung it at the stern. Regarding future measures, Xu Shidao told the New Sound News Agency yesterday that after the Ministry of Communications recovers the wharf, it will prepare to take legal action to recover the rent owed. The matter has now been handled by lawyer Jiang Tianduo. Furthermore, the wharf is now in a terrible state of disrepair due to the damage caused by the Japanese. According to the original regulations, the tenant must repair any damage to the satisfaction of the owner. Because it is in such a bad state today, the Ministry of Communications has instructed the American surveyor Einler to estimate the maximum amount of damage in order to demand compensation from the company.

Yu Da Collision Case Concluded

Foreign Warships Prohibited from Conducting Exercises

Pasten Case Resolved 105

In the case of the collision between the Yu Da steamer and the British submarine Pasten, which was conducting exercises in the waters of Liugong Island in Chengshan Bay, Shandong, the Yu Da shipowner proved that the submarine was at fault. The British naval commander in China also held that the accident was caused by the Pasten's captain, so he dismissed the captain as punishment. Regarding the sunken ship, divers were sent into the sea for inspection. Later, because the seabed at the location of the sinking was very deep, it could not be salvaged. The ship will be temporarily abandoned. The bow of the Yu Da steamer was also damaged and has been repaired. It will continue to sail as usual. The British Navy also believes that the Yu Da steamer is not responsible.

Shipping Association Requests Ban on Naval Exercises 106

After the incident, the Shanghai Shipping Association submitted it to the 14th Executive Committee for discussion. It was agreed that in recent years, British, American, and other foreign warships have often conducted naval exercises within our country's territorial waters, which seriously hinders navigation. As in the Yu Da case, the foreign warships' exercises obstructed the merchant ships. It was resolved that the Shipping Association should submit reasons to the Ministries of Communications and Foreign Affairs, requesting them to inform all countries to prohibit foreign warships and submarines from conducting exercises in our territorial waters in the future, in order to prevent future crises for merchant ships and avoid major disputes.

All Overseas Chinese in Korea are in Grave Danger
